Top 32 Decklists of GP Lyon
===========================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 18, 2018 






![](https://magic.wizards.com/sites/mtg/files/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_FrankKarsten.jpg?itok=KspOJEPD)
By Frank Karsten











There is more to this event than just the [Top 8](https://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gplyo18/top-8-decklists-2018-02-18). Below are the decklists of the players who finished in 9th through 32nd place. All of them were at most one match win and/or a tiebreaker boost away from the Top 8.







#### Berthold La Rocca's Affinity – 9th (13-2) at Grand Prix Lyon 2018


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
